# ED Orientation

**Status.** Living single-file orientation reference for the Event Density (ED) framework. Updated in place as the program evolves вҖ” no version freezing, no v1.x file chain. Last substantive update: 2026-04-23 (seventeenth pass вҖ” F4 Correlation-class sub-arc **CLOSED** via nine-memo arc: canonical Inconclusive (pair sparsity); F4-alt Inconclusive strict / Refuted-by-extension structural (C(r) saturated at ~2 from r=1.0 lu); F4-alt-refine Inconclusive-thin (lattice-discretisation obstruction: О”r < 0.41 lu under-resolves square-ZВІ inter-site distances); F4 Integration memo synthesises three-line verdict).

**Citation form.** Cite by section, not by version. Example: "ED-Orientation В§6.9" for the ED-SC 2.0 invariance statement. If a point-in-time snapshot is ever needed for an external paper citation, use git's commit SHA of this file rather than a version number in the filename.

**How to use.** Read В§1 first (scope + discrepancy map with repo). В§3.1 disambiguates the two P1вҖ“P7 axiom sets (derivation vs. Canon). В§5.9 is the meta-claim (laws / symmetries as emergent). В§6.9 is the current canonical cross-scale invariance statement (ED-SC 2.0). **В§7 is the five-test empirical-status table** with links to all five operational protocols (AFM / UDM-FRAP / ED-09.5 Track A / ED-09.5 Track B / C7 Triad-Coupling). **The Test-to-Axiom Mapping Report at [`docs/ED-Test-to-Axiom-Mapping-v1.0.md`](ED-Test-to-Axiom-Mapping-v1.0.md)** is the 18Г—5 coverage matrix that drove the C7 addition. В§11 is the Emergence-Universe sandbox (pre-ED proof-of-concept). В§2 for the paper trajectory. В§8 for full inventory (Desktop + PhilArchive + GitHub). В§9 for question-type routing.

- **2026-05-02 (ARC Q-COMPUTE CLOSED; QC FOUNDATIONS PAPER PUBLISHED; UR-1 THEOREM ADDED TO INVENTORY).** **Arc Q-COMPUTE closes via seven-memo arc** in `theory/Quantum_Computing/`: Opening (1) + UR-1 derivation (2) + failure-mode rates (3) + architectural-class exhaustiveness audit (4) + multiplicity-cap function $M$ (5) + predictive content (6) + synthesis (7). **UR-1 (Unresolved-Regime Characterization Theorem)** added to structural-theorem inventory (joins T17, T18, T19вҖ“T21+ECR, N1, GR1, DCGT). UR-1 states three independently-necessary substrate conditions for the unresolved-rule regime: (i) multiplicity bounded $\mathcal{M} \leq \mathcal{M}_\mathrm{crit}$; (ii) cross-endpoint connectivity sustained $\gamma_{ij} \geq \Gamma_\mathrm{min}$; (iii) commitment-injection bounded. **Functional form of unresolvedness $\mathcal{U}$:** three-factor product (multiplicity headroom Г— rule-spanning connectivity Г— commitment-survival exponential). Form FORCED; specific shapes of $\mu, \kappa$ INHERITED from V1-kernel + DCGT. **QC operating window:** $\tau_\mathrm{QC} = \min(\tau_{(\mathrm{i})}, \tau_{(\mathrm{ii})}, \tau_{(\mathrm{iii})})$ вҖ” three failure-mode timescales unified. **Three-class architectural exhaustiveness FORCED:** Class A (engineered-low-multiplicity: SC qubits, JJ devices, ions, gate-model photonic вҖ” protects (i) via structural simplification, binds on (ii)/(iii)); Class B (global-geometric-rigidity: topological qubits, photonic Chern channels вҖ” protects (ii) via topological invariants, binds on $\tau_\mathrm{gap-stab}$); Class C (high-multiplicity-redundancy: Hafezi multi-timescale, bosonic codes вҖ” relaxes (i) via redundancy, binds on correlation-budget saturation). Class D candidates (dynamical decoupling, reservoir engineering, error-correction-as-architecture, hybrids) audited and rejected as new classes вҖ” they are *techniques* extending one timescale or *meta-architectural compositions* of A/B/C. **Multiplicity-cap function $M$:** one substrate object with three architectural-class projections plus meta-architectural overlay structure; $M(\mathcal{S}, K, \mathcal{E}, \mathcal{O}) = \min[\tau^{(K,\mathcal{O})}_{(\mathrm{i})}, \tau^{(K,\mathcal{O})}_{(\mathrm{ii})}, \tau^{(K,\mathcal{O})}_{(\mathrm{iii})}]$. **Cross-platform unification вҖ” strongest output:** matter-wave Q-C boundary (140вҖ“250 kDa) and qubit-system multiplicity walls are the *same substrate phenomenon* projected onto two platforms via shared $\mathcal{M}_\mathrm{crit}$. **Sharp predictions:** Class A system-multiplicity wall (no engineering pushes past); Class B exponential gap-suppression $\sim \exp(\Delta_\mathrm{top}/T_\mathrm{eff})$; Class C correlation-budget plateau at $N \sim N_\mathrm{corr}$ (bounded redundancy advantage). **Cross-class transitions:** A вҶ’ C mandatory at the wall; B overtakes A at $\Delta/T \gtrsim 10$вҖ“20; C saturates at $N_\mathrm{corr}$. **Empirical anchors (all clean on $M$):** matter-wave Q-C (Class A static (i) failure); SC qubit TвӮҒ/TвӮӮ (Class A (ii)/(iii) environmental); JJ MQT (Class A engineered (ii) boundary, WKB recovered from DCGT); topological-gap suppression (Class B); Hafezi multi-timescale (Class C, ED-I-18 В§7); bosonic codes (Class C); surface-code logical (Meta: A+C). **Cross-domain echo with BH-2:** $\Gamma_\mathrm{cross}$ collapse mechanism shared with horizon formation; same DCGT machinery at engineered-system scale and gravitational-collapse scale, separated by ~50 orders of magnitude. **Conditional-positive structural verdict** parallel to NS-Smoothness Intermediate Path C, YM Clay-relevance, Arc ED-10, Arc BH. **Q-COMPUTE Foundations Paper published** at `papers/Quantum_Computing_Foundations/` (.md + .tex + .pdf): *"Quantum Computation in Event Density: A Substrate-Level Architecture and Its Limits."* Includes explicit conceptual-shift framing in В§1.4 (decoherence-centric вҶ’ multiplicity-centric reframing) and В§9.6 (roadmap implications: structural-not-technological scaling limits; matter-wave вҶ” qubit-system identity; only Class B can outrun the wall; redundancy saturates; topology-stabilized architectures are the long-term path). Three Foundations papers now form the program's architectural-foundation publication set: SG-Foundations + BH-Foundations + QC-Foundations. **Methodological commitment preserved:** form-FORCED / value-INHERITED across the entire arc; six explicit OPEN extensions named (O-QC-1 closed-form $\mathcal{M}_\mathrm{crit}$; O-QC-2 architecture-to-platform calibration; O-QC-3 closed-form $g/h/c(N)$; O-QC-4 topology-stability theorem; O-QC-5 surface-code recursive overlay; O-QC-6 hybrid-architecture handoff dynamics). **Decisive falsifier:** identification of a QC platform whose coherence behavior is consistent with no class assignment, cannot be explained as meta-architectural composition, and fails to match $M$ under any substrate-allowed parameter calibration would force Class D introduction or framework replacement. **Durable findings (must remain stable across future sessions):** (i) UR-1 is the gate-condition theorem for QC in ED; the unresolved-regime is characterized by three independent-in-form substrate conditions. One condition supports six derivations. **Architectural results FORCED:** horizon = decoupling surface (universal across BH/Rindler/cosmic/acoustic horizons); no singularities (three substrate constraints вҖ” finite participation, discrete micro-events, gradient saturation вҖ” jointly forbid divergence); information blocking + entanglement straddling at horizons; evaporation as participation re-routing through pair-creation events at saturated decoupling surface; area-law entropy form $S = (A/\ell_P^2)\log g$; BHPT phase shift $\delta_{\ell m} = \int_\mathrm{path}\Delta\mathcal{A}\,d\lambda$; helicity preservation/flip; Kerr twist as integrated frame-dragging vorticity. **Standard puzzles not-generated-in-framework rather than solved-within-framework:** the four assumptions generating information paradox / firewall / complementarity / singularity (global unitarity, global Cauchy data, sharp geometric boundary, monogamy-at-boundary) are not imposed at substrate level. The information paradox, firewall paradox, complementarity contradiction, and singularity problem are not solved in ED вҖ” they simply never arise in its ontology. **Value-layer INHERITED:** entropy 1/4 coefficient corresponds to $\log g \approx 1/4$ (with $g \approx 1.28$, non-integer); requires V1 cross-patch correlations to reduce naive integer-$g$ counts; closed-form derivation parallel to closed-form $\mathcal{M}_\mathrm{crit}$ in QC and $\kappa/|\hat{N}'|$ anchor (E4). BHPT spectral details, $\beta_\mathrm{crit}$, V1 kernel width + motif alphabet $g$. **Conditional-positive structural verdict** parallel to NS-Smoothness, YM, Arc ED-10. **Open follow-ons:** Hawking spectrum derivation (B4 вҖ” next natural arc; mechanism in hand from BH-4, load-bearing work is V5 cross-chain correlation calculation); superradiance amplitude (O1); closed-form $\log g$ (O2); full Kerr interior audit (O3). **BH Foundations Paper published** at `papers/Black_Hole_Foundations/` (.md + .tex + .pdf v2): *"Black Holes in Event Density: A Substrate-Level Architecture."* Explicit not-generated-in-framework framing for the four standard paradoxes in В§1.3 + В§10.3. **Durable findings:** (i) horizons are coarse-grained statistical features of $\Gamma_\mathrm{cross}$ collapse, not knife-edge geometric loci; (ii) singularities are breakdowns of the acoustic-metric coarse-grained reading, not of the underlying substrate (substrate dynamics remain finite throughout); (iii) committed structure (information) cannot cross a horizon as participation-bandwidth prohibition, not causal prohibition; uncommitted structure (entanglement) straddles freely; (iv) evaporation = pair-creation-class events at saturated decoupling surface, with one leg committing inward and one outward, joint correlation preserved globally; (v) the four-assumption paradox-generating cluster is not imposed at substrate level вҖ” paradoxes don't arise. **Durable memory:** `memory/project_arc_bh.md` (Arc BH closure, full); `memory/MEMORY.md` index entry; cross-domain $\Gamma_\mathrm{cross}$-collapse echo with QC condition (ii) failure flagged.

FORCED: ПҒ вҶ” Primitive 05 count-density, H = 1вҲ’D. CANDIDATE: D вҶ” ОЈbВІ/(ОЈb)ВІ participation-ratio form, П„ вҶ” participation-bandwidth relaxation timescale. SPECULATIVE: О¶ вҶ” four-band dissipation, v вҶ” polarity-weighted commitment-rate, MвӮҖ, PвӮҖ. Saturation condition committed to joint form `ПҒ > ПҒ_sat AND |вҲҮПҒ| > Оә_sat`. (d) [`quantum/effective_theory/zeta_derivation.md`](../quantum/effective_theory/zeta_derivation.md) вҖ” derives `О¶ = П„В·Оұ_envВ·О“_com/b_com = П„/П„_com` from four-band flux-continuity; shortcut `О¶ = ОӣВ·П„` absorbs microscopic parameters into Hornberger Оӣ; promotes О¶ to CANDIDATE. **For Arndt regime: О¶ вүӘ 1 across all П„ candidates, so `D_crit(О¶_Arndt) вүҲ 0.828` uniformly.** (e) [`quantum/effective_theory/visibility_to_bandwidth.md`](../quantum/effective_theory/visibility_to_bandwidth.md) вҖ” under three CANDIDATE commitments (3-channel KDTLI, sublinear composition exp=2, `b_coh = VВІВ·b_total`), derives `D(V) = VвҒҙ/2 + (1вҲ’VВІ)ВІ` with range `[1/3, 1]`. **Q-C prediction `V_c вүҲ 0.304`** (solving D(V_c) = 0.828). (f) [`quantum/effective_theory/apparatus_envelope.md`](../quantum/effective_theory/apparatus_envelope.md) вҖ” structural decomposition `V_measured = V_env Г— V_coh` (FORCED). Empirical `V_env_Eibenberger вүҲ 0.40`, `V_env_LUMI вүҲ 0.33` from paper's own quantum-prediction curves. First-pass formula-reconstruction off by ~12Г— (convention-sensitivity to Brezger 2003 / Hornberger 2004 factors вҖ” primary refs not retrieved). **Envelope-corrected predictions:** `V_c_measurable(KDTLI) вүҲ 0.122`, `V_c_measurable(LUMI) вүҲ 0.100`. (g) [`quantum/retrodictions/arndt_verdict.md`](../quantum/retrodictions/arndt_verdict.md) вҖ” Eibenberger L12 at ~10,000 amu gives `V_coh вүҲ 0.82`, 2.7Г— the ED boundary. **Verdict: INCONCLUSIVE.** (h) [`quantum/retrodictions/fein2019_verdict.md`](../quantum/retrodictions/fein2019_verdict.md) вҖ” Fein 25 kDa library gives `V_coh вүҲ 0.76`, 2.5Г— the ED boundary. **Verdict: INCONCLUSIVE.** (i) [`quantum/retrodictions/distinguishing_signatures.md`](../quantum/retrodictions/distinguishing_signatures.md) вҖ” proposed N_osc вүҲ 9 / Q вүҲ 3.5 / 3вҖ“6% third-harmonic check surfaces **two structural problems**: (Problem 1) `D < 0.1` unreachable under the D(V) formula (D_min = 1/3); (Problem 2) signatures are likely temporal, not spatial. (j) [`quantum/effective_theory/d_variable_disambiguation.md`](../quantum/effective_theory/d_variable_disambiguation.md) вҖ” **partially resolves Problem 1**: distinguishes `D_P` (participation-ratio, primitive-level, matter-wave-testable) from `D_E` (PDE coupling weight, underdamping-discriminant level, likely temporal-platform-testable). CANDIDATE affine mapping `D_E = (NВ·D_PвҲ’1)/(NвҲ’1)`. Under N=3: Eibenberger and Fein both sit at `D_E < 0.02`, inside the distinguishing-signature regime. V_c prediction survives disambiguation (0.304 вҶ’ 0.302). **Durable quantum-program findings (must remain stable across future sessions):** (i) **Two-point coherence-trajectory extrapolation:** combining Eibenberger (V_coh вүҲ 0.82 at 10 kDa) + Fein (V_coh вүҲ 0.76 at 25 kDa) under envelope-corrected framework yields the ED Q-C boundary at molecular masses **140,000вҖ“250,000 amu** (linear vs exponential extrapolation) вҖ” **5вҖ“10Г— beyond current experimental reach.** This is the first multi-dataset quantitative prediction the program has produced against real data. (ii) **Envelope-correction requirement is structural:** any raw-V vs V_c comparison without envelope correction is systematically misleading. The `V = 0.33` (Eibenberger measured) vs `V_c = 0.304` (ED predicted) numerical coincidence was diagnosed and rejected as apparatus-envelope artifact, not retrodiction match. (iii) **Arndt-group publication pattern:** both Eibenberger 2013 and Fein 2019 report V-vs-laser-power at fixed molecular mass, not V-vs-mass sweeps. Q-C-crossing retrodiction requires either a dataset type not yet published or extrapolation across papers. (iv) **Two D variables exist in the framework.** The Q-C Boundary paper's predictions (N_osc, Q, harmonic) are at D_E; the visibilityвҶ’D map produces D_P. Affine mapping is CANDIDATE; explicit PDE-coarse-graining derivation is Phase-2 work. (v) **Distinguishing signatures likely require temporal-coherence platforms** (cavity QED, superconducting qubits, optomechanics), not matter-wave interferometry, if Problem 2 confirms the signatures are time-domain. **Open blockers (highest-priority first):** (1) **archive read** of [`archive/research_history/ED Physics/ED-Phys-16_CoupledOscillators/`](../archive/research_history/ED%20Physics/ED-Phys-16_CoupledOscillators/) and [`ED-Phys-17_OscillatorCosmology/`](../archive/research_history/ED%20Physics/ED-Phys-17_OscillatorCosmology/) to determine whether the 3вҖ“6% harmonic is spatial (fringe) or temporal (coherence-evolution) вҖ” resolves Problem 2 at lowest cost. (2) Promote the CANDIDATE affine D_P вҶ’ D_E mapping to FORCED via explicit PDE-coarse-graining derivation. (3) Retrieve Brezger 2003 / Hornberger 2004 primary references to resolve the factor-12 envelope-formula discrepancy (empirical V_env readings are currently authoritative). (4) Temporal-coherence platform survey if Problem 2 confirms signatures are temporal. **Guardrails for future sessions:** (i) any quantum-program citation of `D` must specify `D_P` or `D_E`; the Q-C Boundary paper's notation is ambiguous. (ii) any raw-visibility-to-ED-prediction comparison must apply envelope correction `V_measured = V_env Г— V_coh` before comparing to `V_c_raw`. (iii) Eibenberger 2013 and Fein 2019 are consistent-weak-form, not tests; the ED Q-C boundary is beyond current Arndt-apparatus reach. (iv) **Methodological:** proposing a path conceptually and executing it are different acts; the distinguishing-signature path looked viable until execution surfaced Problems 1 and 2. Future next-step recommendations should bias toward the smallest concrete executable step over larger path endorsements. **Program-level decision point at session close:** three options вҖ” (A) archive read (cheapest remediation, high information return), (B) pivot to Path A (QM as thin-regime effective theory, internal theory work), (C) natural stopping point given the program has produced substantial new infrastructure.

- **2026-04-23 (eleventh pass). Scalar r* is re-scoped as the S1 (median) projection of this distribution; r* is a **filtered GRF statistic** whose value depends on (L_ray/Оҫ, Оұ_filt, N_req), not a universal invariant. **Seven authoritative memos (the ED-SC 3.x arc):** [`theory/ED_SC_3_0_Scope.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_0_Scope.md) rev. 2 (distributional architecture + within-regime S-F2 + resonance-mapping clause), [`theory/ED_SC_3_1_rev2_Rectification.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_1_rev2_Rectification.md) (canonical Оҫ anchor + canonical pool), [`theory/ED_SC_3_1_rev3_CanonicalPointCertification.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_1_rev3_CanonicalPointCertification.md) (canonical operating-point certification), [`theory/ED_SC_3_2_LrayXi_Scan.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_2_LrayXi_Scan.md) rev. 2 (coarse hinge scan), [`theory/ED_SC_3_2_5_G3_G4_Transition.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_2_5_G3_G4_Transition.md) (fine-grid plateau map), [`theory/ED_SC_3_2_6_RayBudget_Resonance.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_2_6_RayBudget_Resonance.md) rev. 2 (resonance confirmation + canonical 40-snapshot Оҫ mandate). **Durable structural findings (must remain stable across future sessions):** (a) **Canonical Оҫ anchor** = `1.7575325729470939 lu` (10-seed, 40-snapshot mean, GR-SC 1.7 half-decay on density channel; artefact `outputs/ed_sc_3_1/xi_canonical.json`). Two forbidden windows: **Window A** `L_ray вҲҲ [2.50, 2.80] lu` (вҲҡ4 вҶ’ вҲҡ9 shell transition) and **Window B** `L_ray вҲҲ [3.50, 3.90] lu` (вҲҡ10 вҶ’ вҲҡ16 shell transition). These are structural properties of the filter, not the field. (e) **Within-regime S-F2** вҖ” 20% tolerance applies only within a contiguous regime; cross-regime drifts are diagnostic, not falsifying. - **2026-04-22 (eighth pass).** **Analytic derivation of ED-SC 2.0 `r* = вҲ’1.304` вҖ” four-memo arc, closed-form leading-order asymptotic achieved.** Following the sixth-pass flag ("analytical derivation of `r* = вҲ’1.304` from Scenario D structure"), a four-memo analytic chain now reaches from the Scenario-D PDE to a single-parameter transcendental equation for r*. **Four memos in ascending depth:** (1) [`theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Derivation_Attempt.md`](../theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Derivation_Attempt.md) вҖ” 3-parameter Gaussian+quadrupole ansatz; closed forms `T = вҲ’27ПҖ M_0/8` (trace invariant on pure-peak branch) and large-Оө `r* = вҲ’5/27 вүҲ вҲ’0.185`; target not reproduced; three obstructions identified (saddle vs peak, non-gradient M_2, filter conditioning). (3) [`theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Local_Geometry.md`](../theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Local_Geometry.md) вҖ” works directly with the full 2D nonlinear saddle PDE and FreidlinвҖ“Wentzell quasi-potential; derives the variational obstruction `G[Оҙ] = ВҪ M_2 Оҙ |вҲҮОҙ|ВІ` (makes ОЁ вү  2ОҰ); produces the headline symbolic formula `r* = 4ОјОәвҲҘОәвҠҘ / [ПҖ + 2Ој(ОәвҲҘВІ+ОәвҠҘВІ) вҲ’ M_2 Оҙ_max(ОәвҲҘ+ОәвҠҘ) вҲ’ M_2 рқ’Ұ_NL]` with `Ој = M(Оҙ_max)`, `ПҖ = P'(Оҙ_max)`; flags рқ’Ұ_NL as the single nonlocal scalar correction. (4) [`theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Anisotropy.md`](../theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Anisotropy.md) вҖ” Taylor-expands the saddle PDE to O(rВІ), derives the **anisotropy equation** `12Ој(pвҲ’r) = (aвҲ’b)В·[ПҖ вҲ’ 6M_2 d(a+b)]` (new, local, relates quartic-asymmetry to quadratic-asymmetry); finds the **natural-amplitude closure** `Оҙ_maxВІ = вҲ’6P_0/P_3` at which the cubic nullcline forces the trace to vanish вҶ’ **`s = ОәвҲҘ/ОәвҠҘ = вҲ’1` at leading order** (zero-trace saddle, PDE-level analytic, independent of M_0 and M_2); **produces the first closed-form asymptotic r* = вҲ’2ПҮ/(2ПҮвҲ’1)** with `ПҮ вүЎ 2ОјОәвҠҘВІ/P_0`; matches target `r* = вҲ’1.304 вҹә ПҮ = 2.145 вҹә ОәвҠҘВІ вүҲ 2.14` (physical O(1) motif width in natural units `M_0 = P_0 = |P_3| = 1`). **Durable structural findings (four that must remain stable in future sessions):** (a) **ED-SC 2.0's canonical `r* = вҲ’1.304` is the spatial principal-curvature ratio `ОәвҲҘ/ОәвҠҘ`, not the field-space Hessian ratio `О»_med/ОЈО»`** вҖ” the Extended memo demonstrates these differ at O(1) and the field-space reading gives +0.36 at the best numerical saddle. Update ED-SC 2.0 В§1.4 ambiguity (which "Hessian"): **spatial Hessian K of Оҙ*** at the central stationary point, not field-space Hessian H of ОЁ. (b) **The Scenario-D saddle sits exactly on the cubic nullcline** `Оҙ_maxВІ = вҲ’6P_0/P_3` at leading order; this is what makes the trace `ОәвҲҘ+ОәвҠҘ = 0` and therefore `s = вҲ’1`. The Extended memo's empirical `s вүҲ вҲ’1.304` is a first-order shift `О”s = вҲ’0.304` encoded as `Оө = (Оҙ_maxВІ/(вҲ’6P_0/P_3)) вҲ’ 1` вҖ” a single scalar from the motif's anisotropic tail. (c) **The variational obstruction to ED being gradient flow is explicit and local:** drift differs from `вҲ’ОҙОҰ/ОҙОҙ` by `G[Оҙ] = ВҪ M_2 Оҙ |вҲҮОҙ|ВІ`. ОЁ = 2ОҰ + M_2 ОЁ_1 + O(M_2ВІ); ОЁ_1 transport equation (3.9b of Local Geometry memo) is solvable along instantons from Оҙ=0 to Оҙ*. (d) **Three empirical scalars close the derivation end-to-end:** `ОәвҠҘ` (вҠҘ-decay rate of the saddle), `Оө` (amplitude shift from nullcline), `рқ’Ұ_NL` (M_2 nonlocal correction). - **2026-04-22 (seventh pass).** **External parallel work noted вҖ” Lohmiller & Slotine, "On computing quantum waves exactly from classical action," *Proc. R. Soc. A* 482 (2026) 20250413; arXiv:2405.06328.** SL construct SchrГ¶dinger wave functions exactly from a рқ•Ғ-valued classical least-action field `ПҶ_j(x, t)` plus classical density `ПҒ_j` transported along each extremal branch: `ПҲ_j = вҲҡПҒ_j В· exp(iПҶ_j/в„Ҹ) В· exp(вҲ’ВҪ вҲ«вӮҖбө— О”_M ПҶ_j dОё)`, `ПҲ = ОЈ_j ПҲ_j` (eq. 3.1). **Crucial technical point:** they retain the *pure classical* Hamilton-Jacobi p.d.e. вҖ” **no Bohm quantum potential `Q = вҲ’(в„ҸВІ/2m)вҲҮВІвҲҡПҒ/вҲҡПҒ` is added**. "Quantum" behavior emerges entirely from (i) non-Lipschitz branch points where `О”_M ПҶ_j` is unbounded (generated by multiply-connected manifolds, inequality constraints, singularities, or multi-valued initial data), plus (ii) coherent summation across branches. Lemma 3.1 proves each `ПҲ_j` exactly solves SchrГ¶dinger (1.6); extends to Klein-Gordon / Pauli / Dirac / Maxwell; illustrated via double-slit, Aharonov-Bohm, particle-in-box, tunnelling, hydrogen, harmonic oscillator, EPR/spin. **Relation to ED (calibrated):** independent confirmation that `(density, action-like field)` is the right primitive pair for SchrГ¶dinger recovery вҖ” structurally parallel to ED's `(ПҒ, participation)` pairing in the reversible slice. **Significant differences:** SL is particle-mechanical on `в„қ^N` (not field-theoretic); SL's phase is the classical action satisfying HJ, while ED's participation is *not* an HJ action (relaxational ODE `П„ вҲӮ_t v = F[ПҒ] вҲ’ О¶ v`, part of a triad with saturation and dissipation); SL has no penalty, no mobility channel, no RG flow, no triad closure, no cross-scale invariance. SL claims *exact* SchrГ¶dinger/KG/Pauli/Dirac equivalence; ED claims only *reversible-slice consistency* with free scalar QFT (per `memory/project_ed10_geometry_qft_scope.md` guardrails). Both treat QM as *recovered*, not *axiomatic*. **Status:** calibrated citation added to [`theory/ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md В§8`](../theory/ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md); SL should be cited as parallel external evidence for the density + action-like-field decomposition, **not** as evidence for any ED-specific claims (triad, RG closure, cross-scale invariance `r* = вҲ’1.304`, penalty saturation). **Speculative transferable tool** (flagged, not adopted): SL's branch-indexed mechanism вҖ” extremal action branches + `exp(вҲ’ВҪ вҲ« О”_M ПҶ dОё)` amplitude factor + coherent sum вҖ” could be examined for whether ED's participation field admits an analogous multi-branch construction along ED-SC 2.0's ray-extremal motifs. No ED doc or prediction changes on the strength of SL.

- **2026-04-22 (sixth pass).** **Wilsonian RG analysis of the canonical ED PDE completed вҖ” five memos closing the coarse-graining / flow-geometry / UV / IR / three-regime arc, plus the 0.6 problem resolution.** Math-only theoretical push following the ED-10 geometry closure. **Five durable structural results that must remain stable across future sessions:** (a) **ED operator basis is form-closed under Wilsonian coarse-graining.** At tree level and one loop, no operators outside `{M(ПҒ)вҲҮВІПҒ + M'(ПҒ)|вҲҮПҒ|ВІ, P(ПҒ), П„ vМҮ, О¶ v, H v, D F[Оҙ]}` are generated. (b) **ED is NOT an RG fixed point at physical couplings.** At dynamic exponent `z = 2`: `ОІ_{M_0} = 0` (marginal), `ОІ_{P_0} = 2P_0`, `ОІ_О¶ = 2О¶`, `ОІ_П„ = вҲ’2П„`, `ОІ_{P_3} = (2вҲ’2ПҮ)P_3`, `ОІ_{M_2} = вҲ’2ПҮ M_2`. (d) **Two crossover scales bound the "ED window"** вҖ” `в„“_v = ВҪ ln(Оҫ_v Оӣ)` (participation-slaving onset) and `в„“_Оҫ = ln(Оҫ Оӣ)` (gap-dominated scale). ED-specific phenomenology (Q-C transition, C7 triad coupling, UDM ОІ=2, saturating penalty) lives in `в„“_v < в„“ < в„“_Оҫ` only. (e) **Three-regime effective PDE structure, each regime boxed in the authoritative memos:** **UV** `вҲӮ_t Оҙ = D M_0 вҲҮВІОҙ + H v,  П„ vМҮ = M_0 вҲҮВІОҙ` (free two-channel diffusion; v frozen at `П„ вҶ’ вҲһ`; wave-like dispersion вҖ” this is the kinematic acoustic-metric / free-scalar QFT regime from the fourth-pass arc). **Intermediate** `вҲӮ_t Оҙ = О“_eff [M_0 вҲҮВІОҙ + (M_2/2) ОҙВІвҲҮВІОҙ + M_2 Оҙ|вҲҮОҙ|ВІ вҲ’ P_0 Оҙ вҲ’ (P_3/6) ОҙВі]` with `О“_eff = D + H/О¶` (participation slaved, Model A universality). **IR** `вҲӮ_t Оҙ = D M_0 вҲҮВІОҙ вҲ’ D P_0(в„“) Оҙ,  P_0(в„“) вҶ’ вҲһ` (linear gapped diffusion; Оҙ вҶ’ 0 exponentially; two-stage nonlinearity elimination). **Cross-scale invariance re-stated honestly:** the "ED across 20-60 OOM" claim is not coupling-invariance вҖ” couplings flow. It is **operator-structure invariance** within the intermediate window. Window location and coupling values are regime-specific. **The 0.6 problem closed in the same pass:** `0.6 = 2В·D_nd(quantum)` as a structural dictionary identity, derived from `T_0 = L_0ВІВ·D_nd/D_phys` with `D_phys = в„Ҹ/(2m)` (Madelung theorem) and `L_0 = в„Ҹ/(mc)` (reduced Compton) вҶ’ `T_0 = 2В·D_ndВ·в„Ҹ/(mcВІ) = 0.6В·в„Ҹ/(mcВІ)`. Five alternative routes audited (damping discriminant, reversible-slice QFT dispersion, acoustic-metric curvature, PME coarse-graining, О¶-interpolation) вҖ” all fail. - **2026-04-22 (third pass).** **D_crit discrepancy resolved вҖ” Canon P6 single-number `D_crit = 0.5` retired in favour of the О¶-parametrised linearised form.** Full derivation in [`theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md`](../theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md). Linearising the canonical PDE around homogeneous equilibrium, Fourier-decomposing, and evaluating the 2Г—2 coupled-eigenvalue discriminant yields the underdamping condition `(D вҲ’ О¶)ВІ < 4(1 вҲ’ D)` at reference mode `Оө_kВ·П„ = 1`, with critical threshold **`D_crit(О¶) = вҲҡ(2вҲ’О¶)В·(2 вҲ’ вҲҡ(2вҲ’О¶))`**. At canon-default `О¶ = 1/4`, `D_crit вүҲ 0.896`. At `О¶ = 0`, `D_crit = 2вҲҡ2 вҲ’ 2 вүҲ 0.828`. At `О¶ вҶ’ 1`, `D_crit вҶ’ 1`. **The 00.2 Canon P6 heuristic `О” = D + 2О¶, critical at О” = 1 вҶ’ D_crit = 1 вҲ’ 2О¶ = 0.5`** is not recoverable as any principled limit of the full discriminant (attempting to match via Оө-rescaling yields the quadratic `4ОөВІ вҲ’ 36Оө + 1 = 0` with roots ~8.97 and ~0.028, neither at the canonical `Оө = 1`). **Root cause of the heuristic's ~80% error:** the additive form drops the coupled cross-term `(D вҲ’ О¶)ВІ` of the true discriminant, flips the sign of the cross-coupling (replacing `вҲ’2DО¶` with `+4DО¶`), and over-weights `О¶` by ~2Г—. **Ruled out as sources of the discrepancy:** dimensionality (per-mode eigenvalue problem is scalar in any `d`), mobility form (enters only via `MвӮҖ = M(ПҒ*)` at linear order вҖ” ОІ=1, ОІ=2, SY2 all identical at linear order), penalty form (both linear and SY2 linearise to `PвӮҖВ·ОҙПҒ`), definitional ambiguity (both forms use `traceВІ = 4В·det`). **Regime A (D=1, H=0, mobility-penalty only) has О» = вҲ’Оө_k вҲҲ в„қ<0** вҖ” unconditionally overdamped, `D_crit` not defined in that regime. **Regime B (0<D<1) is where Canon P6 lives** and where the corrected formula applies. **Three verification hooks pass** (limits at О¶=0, О¶=1, monotonicity in О¶). В§3 Canon P6 row and В§4 three-regimes table updated. The "highest-priority v0.5+ theory issue" flagged 2026-04-20 in [`theory/ED-Dimensional-01-Ext.md`](../theory/ED-Dimensional-01-Ext.md) Appendix A is closed.

В§6.10 captures the **Factor Skyline evaluation** (X5D). В§8 inventory updated вҖ” all `ED Important Papers/` files are now `вң“ read`. ED-Dimensional-01 Quantum's **superluminal `V_0 = c/(2В·0.3) вүҲ 1.667c`** is explicitly flagged as a consequence of the parabolic PDE's infinite propagation speed (same property as the SchrГ¶dinger equation) вҖ” it is a scale conversion factor, not a signal speed. No new empirical results; this is a documentation-absorption update.

- **2026-04-20.** **AFM dewetting empirical track is now ED's highest-certainty near-term test.** ED-SC 2.0 В§3 specifies a sharp falsification criterion for the motif-conditioned median of the field-space Hessian on 2D scalar density fields: `med(в„ӣ_motif(h(x,y))) вҲҲ [вҲ’1.50, вҲ’1.10]` for thin-film polymer dewetting in the spinodal pre-rupture regime. Standard AFM resolutions (50 nm lateral, 0.1 nm vertical) satisfy the В§3 sampling requirement `О”x вүӨ L_coh/8` by construction. **Pilot result (N=1, в„ӣ_all not в„ӣ_motif):** Scenario D simulation and one thin-film pilot frame agree at median = вҲ’2.063 vs вҲ’2.149, with overlapping IQRs ([вҲ’3.43, вҲ’1.49] vs [вҲ’3.96, вҲ’1.47]) and matching % in target band (21.7% vs 23.0%). Real AFM data with `L_coh вүҘ ~16 px` would unlock the motif filter. **Three routes to data, in increasing cost and certainty:** (1) browser-check 2023 *Nature Comm Phys* paper for accessible AFM data вҖ” 5 minutes; (2) email Jacobs group вҖ” second-cheapest, builds field connections; (3) book a 1вҖ“2 day session at any academic core facility with PS-on-Si dewetting samples вҖ” guaranteed canonical data by construction. **This is structurally separate from the ED-09.5 / Aspelmeyer / FRAP empirical track** вҖ” it tests ED-SC 2.0 (architectural invariants), not the Q-C transition. ED now has two independent empirical tracks running. **Operational recommendation:** execute Route 1 immediately; chain to 2/3 based on what Route 1 returns. AFM is the highest-certainty empirical path because it has a guaranteed-success physical-acquisition fallback (Route 3) that doesn't depend on any third party. New row added to В§7 empirical-status table. **Route 3 is now operationalized** in [`AFM-Dewetting protocol`](../experiements/AFM-Dewetting-ED-SC_InProcess/protocol.md) вҖ” a session-ready canonical protocol (captured 2026-04-21) covering sample prep, scan parameters, data export, pre-analysis quality gates (including the pilot's root-cause fix: the `L_coh вүҘ 8В·О”x` sampling condition verified per-frame), ensemble statistics, and a five-outcome decision tree (PASS / NEAR-PASS / FAIL / UNDECIDABLE / SPLIT). Budget: ~$500 + ~2 weeks analysis for a complete N=5 samples Г— 10 frames run. Expected timeline to publishable result: 4вҖ“6 weeks from protocol adoption.

---

**Purpose.** This document captures ED framework content that lives **outside the repo** вҖ” in PhilArchive publications and in the user's local `Desktop/ED Interpretations/` and `Desktop/ED Important Papers/` folders вҖ” so that a new Claude Code session can acclimate in one read rather than rediscovering the scope from first principles. The repo is heavily focused on the PDE canon, UDM, merger-lag, and the dimensional atlas; the material below is *complementary* and sometimes *updates* what the repo says.

**The ED framework has three parallel tracks** that the repo does not make visible:

1. **The empirical physics program.** PDE canon вҶ’ dimensional atlas вҶ’ empirical tests in five regimes (quantum, Planck, condensed matter, galactic, cosmological). Concrete predictions, concrete falsification criteria. Lives mostly in the repo (UDM, Cluster Merger-Lag) and in 00.1 / 00.2 / 00.3 / ED-02 / ED-04 / ED-XX from the Desktop PDFs.
2. **The interpretive / ontological program.** Reframes existing phenomena in quantum mechanics, optics, information, topology, and spacetime itself as structural consequences of ED participation geometry. Produces structural *explanations*, not new measurements. Lives in ED-10 (spacetime emergence), the ED-I-XX interpretation series (photonics, quantum info, topology, weak lensing), and the PhilArchive philosophical papers (ED-06 / ED-07 / ED-08 / ED-09 / ED-09.5 / ED-13).
3. **The scale-correspondence program (ED-SC).** Identifies architectural invariants that recur across 20+ orders of magnitude. Treats micro вҶ” macro correspondences as structural **identity**, not analogy. Lives in ED-SC-XX and the forthcoming scale-free atlas. First paper: ED-SC-00 (March 2026). See В§6.6.

All three tracks share the same PDE canon and ontology (becoming, micro-events, participation, ED gradients). They differ in their goal: the empirical track tries to *predict* new measurements; the interpretive track tries to *unify* existing ones under one ontology; the scale-correspondence track tries to *identify architectural invariants* that persist when scale, mechanism, and substrate change.

**How to use this at session start.** Read В§1 (scope & discrepancy map) first вҖ” it is the critical information. В§3.1 (the two P1вҖ“P7 axiom sets вҖ” critical disambiguation) prevents confusing derivation axioms with the Canon. В§5.9 (Architecture of Physical Law) is the **meta-claim** behind all three ED tracks: laws and symmetries are emergent, not fundamental. В§6 (ED-XX environment sourcing revision) is the most important empirical-track update. В§6.5 (Interpretation Series vocabulary) is the most important interpretive-track update. В§11 (Emergence-Universe / ED-SIM sandbox) is the pre-ED proof-of-concept for the architecture-first thesis вҖ” disambiguate from the continuum `edsim/` solver. Skim В§2вҖ“5 for depth. В§7 is the empirical status snapshot. В§8 is the full paper / code / GitHub map. В§9 is the step-by-step checklist + question-type map. В§12 is the non-physics Factor Skyline thread (kept for completeness, not session-start reading).

### Things where the repo is authoritative and current

- The canonical PDE algebra (`theory/PDE.md`) вҖ” mobility, penalty, participation channels.
- UDM / mobility channel empirical fit (10 soft-matter materials, RВІ > 0.986).
- Cluster Merger-Lag evidence (7-cluster sample + Finner aggregate).
- Dimensional Atlas (5-regime mapping, DВ·TвӮҖ/LвӮҖВІ = 0.3 invariant).
- Edsim simulation engine.
- Our work this session: RLC analogue memo, BTFR-Activity unified analysis, Finner-A1 test, scale-dependence scoping, etc.

### Discrepancies you should know about at session start

1. **Penalty form.** The repo's `theory/PDE.md` uses the linear `PвӮҖ(ПҒвҲ’ПҒ*)` form. The current canonical form per [00.3] is `P_SY2`. These agree near equilibrium but diverge at the mobility ceiling, and the horizon/heat-death arguments in [00.1] depend on SY2's saturation. If a future session touches `theory/PDE.md`, flag this before editing.
2. **What "D" means.** In repo code and repo docs, `D` is dimensional diffusivity (mВІ/s). In [00.2 Canon] and [00.3 Unified PDE], `D` is the dimensionless channel weight (with `D+H=1`). Context-sensitive.
3. **Galaxy-sourced vs. environment-sourced.** Any repo text or paper that asserts "galaxies generate their own temporal-tension halos" reflects the preвҖ“April-2026 view. [ED-XX] supersedes this вҖ” galaxies set the *amplitude* via baryonic identity, the *spatial extent* comes from the cosmic web.

## 2. The trajectory (dated papers, in order)

The ED main series is numbered **ED-01 through ED-13** (with ED-04.5 and ED-09.5 as half-steps). The main series is complemented by the **00-series** (foundational cosmology math), the **ED-I series** (interpretive applications to quantum / optical / topological phenomena), the **ED-SC series** (scale-correspondence), the **ED-Arch / ED-Sim series** (architectural-invariants + Emergence-Universe sandbox; see В§6.8 and В§11), and the **ED-XX** revision. The Cluster Merger-Lag, Universal Degenerate-Mobility, and Open Note papers are empirical / methodological publications. The two **Factor Skyline** papers are a **separate non-physics thread** on multiplicative number theory (see В§12 вҖ” kept in the inventory because Allen authors them, not because they are ED physics).

Finds a saddle-shaped phase-exit surface with peak at `(n=2.7, Пғ=0.0556)`, step 457. Curvature ratio Оә_вҲҘ/Оә_вҠҘ вүҲ вҲ’1.3 Вұ 0.2 matches the Local Group mass sheet and Casimir cavity. Four regimes empirically identified. **Does NOT contain the 1/r dilution argument.** See В§6.8. |
| **March 2026** | ED-Arch-02 | Architectural Foundations of Event Density | Theoretical counterpart to ED-Arch-01. Defines saddle / channel / boundary / horizon via Hessian geometry (gradient sign-flip, det(H)=0 curves, О»_вҠҘ > 0 for boundaries, О»_вҠҘ < 0 for horizons). Derives universality (IC-independence, parameter-deformation stability, noise-threshold robustness, mobility-law invariance, curvature-driven necessity). See В§6.8. |
| **April 2026** | ED-XX | Environment Sourcing of Temporal Tension | Major revision. Galaxy-sourced hypothesis overturned by a 3D Green's-function `1/r` dilution argument. **Source document NOT located** вҖ” it is NOT ED-SIM-3D, NOT ED-Sim-01 / ED-Arch-01, NOT ED-Arch-02. Likely lives inside the ED-XX paper itself. |
| (in repo) | Cluster Merger-Lag | Cluster Merger-Lag Evidence | 7-cluster sample + Finner aggregate test `в„“ = D_T/v_current`. Currently the primary-cited empirical penalty-channel test. |

**Separate thread вҖ” not part of the ED physics program:** Regulated Multiplicity: An Architectural Account of Consciousness (Dec 2025) and Regulated Multiplicity: An AI Systems Architecture (Jan 2026). Confirmed independently as philosophy-of-mind / AI systems work with no physics content.

## 3. The Architectural Canon (7 principles) вҖ” P1 through P7

From [00.2 March 2026]. Any PDE satisfying these is "architecturally ED," regardless of functional form.

| # | Principle | Statement |
|---|---|---|
| **P1** | Operator Structure | `F[ПҒ] = M(ПҒ)вҲҮВІПҒ + M'(ПҒ)\|вҲҮПҒ\|ВІ вҲ’ P(ПҒ)` вҖ” curvature-dependent diffusion + nonlinear gradient + restoring force |
| **P2** | Channel Complementarity | `ПҒМҮ = DВ·F[ПҒ] + HВ·v`, `D + H = 1`, `D,H вҲҲ [0,1]` вҖ” direct + mediated channels, convex weighting |
| **P3** | Penalty Equilibrium | `P(ПҒ*) = 0` with `P' > 0` вҖ” unique globally-attracting equilibrium |
| **P4** | Mobility Capacity Bound | `M(ПҒ_max) = 0` with `M(ПҒ) > 0` for `ПҒ < ПҒ_max` вҖ” horizon at the capacity bound |
| **P5** | Participation Feedback Loop | `vМҮ = (1/П„)(F[ПҒ] вҲ’ О¶v)` вҖ” memory channel with exponential decay |
| **P6** | Damping Discriminant | **Linearised form (resolved 2026-04-22, [`theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md`](../theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md)):** underdamped iff `(D вҲ’ О¶)ВІ < 4(1 вҲ’ D)` at reference mode `Оө_kВ·П„ = 1`; critical threshold `D_crit(О¶) = вҲҡ(2вҲ’О¶)В·(2 вҲ’ вҲҡ(2вҲ’О¶))`; at canon-default `О¶ = 1/4`, **`D_crit вүҲ 0.896`** (NOT 0.5). The earlier additive heuristic `О” = D + 2О¶, critical at О” = 1 вҶ’ D_crit = 0.5` is retired as quantitative claim (error ~80%); retained only as order-of-magnitude mnemonic. |
| **P7** | Nonlinear Triad Coupling | `M'(ПҒ)В·\|вҲҮПҒ\|ВІ` generates k=3 from k=1 with invariant triad ratio. **Calibrated 2026-04-22** вҖ” scale-free invariant `K = AвӮғ/AвӮҒВі вүҲ 0.0148 Вұ 0.0005`, companion `KвӮӮ = AвӮӮ/AвӮҒВІ вүҲ 0.279`, cubic scaling slope `ОұвӮғ = 3.0 Вұ 0.05`, exact phase lock `ПҶвӮғ вҲ’ 3ПҶвӮҒ = ПҖ` (SD ~ 10вҒ»вҒ¶ rad), symmetry ordering `AвӮӮ > AвӮғ` in the clean regime (~200Г— at AвӮҒ=0.1 per simulation). The amplitude-dependent ratio `AвӮғ/AвӮҒ` is NOT the invariant; the previously-cited ED-Phys-16 "3вҖ“6%" band reproduces only in the saturation regime at `AвӮҒ вүі 0.15В·ПҒ_max`. Operational test: [`experiements/Triad-Coupling-C7_InProcess/protocol.md`](../experiements/Triad-Coupling-C7_InProcess/protocol.md). |

Counterfactual analysis: removing any principle breaks a specific architectural layer (motifs / laws / geometry / invariants). The Canon is minimal and irreducible.

**Why this matters for me:** when I read repo docs that refer to "the ED PDE," I now know this is shorthand for the equivalence class defined by P1вҖ“P7. The specific mobility and penalty forms in `theory/PDE.md` are one instance. The RLC-analogue memo I wrote derives P6 (damping discriminant) in dimensional units without knowing it was P6 вҖ” worth cross-linking if I revisit it. **P7 addendum (2026-04-22):** the Triad-Coupling-C7 simulation companion at [`analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md`](../analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md) reduced P7 from a qualitative "k=3-from-k=1" claim to a sharp four-observable invariant (`K, KвӮӮ, ОұвӮғ, О”ПҶ`). The historical `AвӮғ/AвӮҒ вҲҲ [0.02, 0.08]` band inherited from ED-Phys-16 is retired as a primary criterion; `K = AвӮғ/AвӮҒВі` is the replacement scale-free invariant. The "AвӮӮ < AвӮғ by odd symmetry" claim in earlier drafts of the C7 protocol was **inverted** вҖ” the quadratic `MвҖІ(ПҒ)|вҲҮПҒ|ВІ` sources the second harmonic directly via the DC + 2k structure of `|вҲҮПҒ|ВІ`, so `AвӮӮ > AвӮғ` in the clean regime.

### 3.1 The two P1вҖ“P7 axiom sets вҖ” critical disambiguation

**There are TWO distinct "P1вҖ“P7" axiom sets in the ED corpus, used at different layers of the theory.** Prior Claude sessions have conflated them. When reading any ED document that references "P1" through "P7," first determine which set is being invoked:

| Set | Source | Purpose | Symbol for what's constrained |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **Derivation axioms** | `ED_Foundational_Paper(.md / v2.md)` В§2.4, `ED-Math-01_Uniqueness_Well-Posedness_and_Architectural_Laws.md` Theorem 2.1, `WHAT_IS_ED.md` | Axioms from which the canonical PDE is **derived**. These determine *what the PDE must look like*. Theorem 2.1 proves the canonical ED PDE is the unique second-order scalar PDE satisfying all seven. | P1 = Locality В· P2 = Isotropy В· P3 = Gradient-driven flow В· P4 = Dissipative structure В· P5 = Single scalar field В· P6 = Minimal coupling В· P7 = Dimensional consistency |
| **Architectural Canon (00.2)** | `00.2 Architectural Canon of the Unified ED Cosmology PDE`, `Desktop/ED Important Papers/The Architectural Canon...pdf` | Principles defining ED as a **class** of PDEs. These specify *what structural features every architecturally-ED PDE must have*. Any PDE satisfying these is "architecturally ED," regardless of specific functional forms. | P1 = Operator Structure В· P2 = Channel Complementarity (D+H=1) В· P3 = Penalty Equilibrium В· P4 = Mobility Capacity Bound В· P5 = Participation Feedback Loop В· P6 = Damping Discriminant (D_crit = 0.5) В· P7 = Nonlinear Triad Coupling |

**They are complementary, not contradictory.** The derivation axioms operate at the level of PDE *form* (what mathematical objects are allowed to appear); the Canon principles operate at the level of PDE *architecture* (what structural relations must hold among those objects). A PDE satisfying only the derivation axioms might not be "architecturally ED" unless it also satisfies the Canon; a PDE satisfying the Canon principles has, by construction, the canonical form the derivation axioms produce.

**The ED-13 "seven axioms" claim** ("four primitives and seven axioms uniquely determine the equation") most naturally refers to the **derivation-axiom set** (ED-Math-01 Theorem 2.1), composed with the four ED-05 pre-PDE axioms (non-negativity, null baseline, monotonicity, subadditivity). The 00.2 Canon is a *structural characterization* of what the derivation yields, not an independent set of axioms layered on top.

**When an ED paper says "P4":**
- If the paper is the Foundational Paper, ED-Math-01, or any uniqueness-theorem context вҶ’ P4 = Dissipative structure.
- If the paper is 00.2, 00.3, any "Canon" context, or any paper citing `D_crit = 0.5` вҶ’ P4 = Mobility Capacity Bound.
- **If in doubt, check which set of seven labels appears nearby.** The two sets have no overlapping labels.

The three-track structure documented at the top of this doc (Empirical / Interpretive / Scale-correspondence) generally uses whichever axiom set is most convenient for the current abstraction layer. Both sets are correct; neither is deprecated.

### 3.2 Axioms stack: four ED-05 вҶ’ seven derivation вҶ’ seven Canon

For session-start reference, the full axiom stack from pre-PDE to architectural:

1. **Pre-PDE layer (ED-05, Feb 2026, 4 axioms on a bare event domain):** non-negativity, null baseline, monotonicity, subadditivity. No time, geometry, or probability presupposed.
2. **Derivation layer (Foundational Paper / ED-Math-01, 7 axioms):** locality, isotropy, gradient-driven flow, dissipative structure, single scalar field, minimal coupling, dimensional consistency. ED-Math-01 Theorem 2.1: these **uniquely determine** the canonical PDE up to the choice of constitutive functions `M(ПҒ)` and `P(ПҒ)`.
3. **Architectural Canon layer (00.2, 7 principles):** operator structure, channel complementarity, penalty equilibrium, mobility capacity bound, participation feedback loop, damping discriminant, nonlinear triad coupling. Specifies the structural *architecture* the derived PDE must exhibit.

A PDE that passes all 4+7+7 is guaranteed to reproduce the ED phenomenology: unique attractor, Lyapunov dissipation, three-stage convergence, oscillation-death at D_crit = 0.5, and the 22-correspondence scale-invariance of ED-SC Table 1.

## 4. The Unified Cosmological Equation (00.3 canon)

The canonical PDE in its current cleanest form:

$$\partial_t \rho = D \cdot F[\rho] + H \cdot v, \qquad D + H = 1$$
$$\partial_t v = \frac{1}{\tau}(F[\rho] - \zeta v)$$
$$F[\rho] = M(\rho)\nabla^2\rho + M'(\rho)|\nabla\rho|^2 - P_{SY2}(\rho)$$
$$P_{SY2}(\rho) = \alpha\gamma \cdot \frac{\rho - \rho^*}{\sqrt{(\rho-\rho^*)^2 + \rho_0^2}}$$

### Three regimes (parameter-determined)

| Regime | Condition (heuristic boundaries, 00.3) | Corrected boundary (2026-04-22) | Behavior |
|---|---|---|---|
| Oscillatory | `D < 0.1` | `D вүӘ D_crit(О¶)` вҖ” well below threshold | Underdamped, reversible, standing participation waves, 8вҖ“19 transient oscillations |
| Transitional / Hybrid | `0.1 вүӨ D вүӨ 0.4` | `D вҶ’ D_crit(О¶)` from below | Mixed behavior, smooth interpolation |
| Parabolic | `D вүҘ 0.5` | `D вүҘ D_crit(О¶) вүҲ 0.896` at canon-default `О¶ = 1/4` | Overdamped, irreversible, structure-forming, peak merging, basin formation |

**Note (2026-04-22):** The original heuristic boundaries (`< 0.1`, `0.1вҖ“0.4`, `вүҘ 0.5`) were calibrated against the retired `D_crit = 0.5` heuristic. Full linearised analysis places the parabolic/hybrid boundary at `D_crit(О¶) вүҲ 0.9` (canon-default). The qualitative three-regime structure survives; the numerical boundaries shift upward by ~0.4 in D. Downstream papers (ED-SIM-3D В§6.7, Extended Atlas В§5вҖ“В§7) that used the 0.5 threshold as a regime marker should be re-examined. See [`theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md`](../theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md) В§10.

### Universal invariants

- **Equilibrium density** `ПҒ*` вҖ” unique zero of P_SY2, globally attracting across all D вҲҲ [0,1].
- **Ground state energy** `E_ground = ОұОіПҒвӮҖ` вҖ” independent of dimension, mixing ratio, IC.
- **Relaxation timescale** `t_rel вүҲ ПҒвӮҖ/(ОұОі)` вҖ” varies only ~13% across the entire hybrid parameter space.
- **Horizon behavior** вҖ” near `ПҒ_max`, mobility collapses (diffusion vanishes), but participation v and its inertia survive. This produces oscillating horizons in the oscillatory regime (lifetime extended by ~60%) and collapsing horizons in the parabolic regime.

### Nonlinear structure (weakly coupled)

- Triad resonance `k_3 = k_1 Вұ k_2`, coupling **~0.03 (provenance unclear; ED-Phys-16 fit at undocumented N)**. See [`analysis/ED_SC_2_0_Sample_Size_Audit.md`](../analysis/ED_SC_2_0_Sample_Size_Audit.md) В§2.2. The C7 deterministic-canonical-operator result ([`analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md`](../analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md)) gives `K = AвӮғ/AвӮҒВі = 0.0148 Вұ 0.0005` on a fixed monochromatic IC; whether K and the "0.03" refer to the same object is an open provenance question.
- Harmonic generation at **3вҖ“6% of fundamental (provenance unclear; requires citation or re-run)**. The C7-derived form `AвӮғ/AвӮҒ = KВ·AвӮҒВІ` with K = 0.0148 gives 3% at AвӮҒ вүҲ 1.4 and is the preferred successor statement.
- No mode locking, no chaos, no bifurcations.
- ED is "a weakly nonlinear, weakly coupled, nearly non-dispersive oscillator lattice with reversible participation dynamics."

## 5. The ontology (ED-10 emergence map)

Becoming is primitive. Micro-events are atomic units. Participation is the relational substrate. Everything geometric / informational / temporal is emergent.

### Coarse-graining dictionary

| Classical concept | ED substrate |
|---|---|
| Space | stable participation adjacency |
| Time | commitment order (irreversible) |
| Distance | participation resistance |
| Curvature | ED gradient structure |
| Locality | thick participation coherence |
| Mass / energy | patterns of committed micro-events |
| Horizons | decoupling surfaces / participation bottlenecks |
| Einstein's equations | **not** emergent from ED. Only a kinematic acoustic metric `g^eff_ОјОҪ = diag(вҲ’M(ПҒ_0), 1, 1, 1)` arises (ii-grade, slaved to `ПҒ_0`, no field equation). Schwarzschild unreachable under any coordinate transformation. See [`ED_Effective_Acoustic_Metric.md`](../theory/ED_Effective_Acoustic_Metric.md) + [`ED_Schwarzschild_Obstruction.md`](../theory/ED_Schwarzschild_Obstruction.md). |
| SchrГ¶dinger evolution | **not** derived from ED. In the reversible slice (`D = 0, О¶ = 0`), linearised ED is a free massive Klein-Gordon field whose canonical quantisation is consistent with SchrГ¶dinger-picture free-scalar QFT вҖ” a consistency result, not a derivation of QM. See [`ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md`](../theory/ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md). |
| Wavefunction collapse | irreversible selection of a participation channel |
| Born rule | participation weights |
| Entanglement | shared uncommitted participation structure |
| Information | constraint on viable commitment histories |
| Holography | constraint imposed by decoupling surfaces |
| Entropy | distribution of viable commitment histories |
| Arrow of time | asymmetry of commitment (ontological, not statistical) |

### Continuum

Quantum вҶ’ Relational вҶ’ Classical вҶ’ Geometric. One substrate (participation), regime-dependent expressions.

**Note on scope.** ED-10 is philosophical/architectural, not empirically discriminating. The empirical program lives in the mobility / penalty / participation tests. ED-10 is what makes the framework a *unifying ontology* rather than just a DM alternative, but claims like "the measurement problem dissolves" are interpretive, not tested.

## 5.5 The ED main series вҖ” additional papers (ED-03, ED-05 through ED-09.5, ED-13)

These are PhilArchive-only papers that fill in the conceptual spine of the framework *between* the founding paper (ED-02) and the mature canon (00.2 / 00.3 / ED-XX). Each is summarized here at the level a future session needs to navigate without re-reading.

### ED-05 вҖ” Mathematical Formalization (Feb 2026) вҖ” the pre-PDE axiomatic layer

*Beneath* the PDE canon: a measure-theoretic / categorical structure defining "ED" as a mathematical object before any dynamics are attached.

Four governing axioms on a bare event domain, assigning non-negative density values to finite configurations of events:

1. **Non-negativity** вҖ” ED is always вүҘ 0.
2. **Null baseline** вҖ” the empty configuration has ED = 0.
3. **Monotonicity** вҖ” adding events does not decrease ED.
4. **Subadditivity** вҖ” `ED(A вҲӘ B) вүӨ ED(A) + ED(B)`, capturing the non-linear relational character of becoming.

No time, geometry, causality, or probability is presupposed. **Morphisms between ED systems** are defined to identify when two systems share underlying structure (categorical perspective).

**Relationship to the 00.2 Architectural Canon:** the Canon's P1вҖ“P7 sit at the PDE layer; ED-05's four axioms sit at the pre-PDE layer. ED-13 claims "four primitives and seven axioms" uniquely determine the dynamical equation вҖ” this is the composition of ED-05's four axioms (or the four ontological primitives: micro-events, ED gradients, participation, commitment) with the seven Canon principles.

### ED-06 вҖ” Horizons as Decoupling Surfaces (Feb 2026)

All horizons are manifestations of the same structural phenomenon: **discontinuities in the ED field where gradients become so steep that participation can no longer be reconciled across a boundary**. The flow of becoming becomes one-way.

Unifies:
- Black hole horizons
- Rindler horizons (accelerated observers)
- Cosmological horizons

In each case, "falling behind the horizon" is *participation decoupling*, not geometric crossing. No information paradox: the network splits into disconnected regions; nothing "falls into" anything. Thermal behavior (Hawking / Unruh temperature) arises from gradient steepness at the boundary, not from field-theoretic pair creation.

**Consistent with** ED-10 В§4.4 and 00.1 В§8.3, which use the same decoupling-surface framing.

### ED-07 вҖ” Relativistic Phenomena (Feb 2026)

Relativistic phenomena emerge from the architecture of becoming, not from a fundamental spacetime geometry:

| Relativistic phenomenon | ED mechanism |
|---|---|
| Invariance of `c` | `c` = maximum rate at which causal updates propagate through the ED network |
| Time dilation | Differences in local rate of becoming |
| Length contraction | Participation-adjacency compression along a motion direction |
| Redshift | Cumulative participation stretching across ED gradients |
| Inertial motion | Gradient-minimizing participation pathway |
| Curvature | Macroscopic imprint of uneven ED flow |
| Lorentz symmetry | Structural consequence of participation architecture |
| Geodesics | Stable participation pathways |

Does *not* modify GR's field equations; reframes what sources them. `c` being an invariant is derived here, not assumed вҖ” which is a stronger claim than GR makes.

### ED-08 вҖ” Cosmological Structure: Temporal Tension and Expansion (Feb 2026)

Complements 00.1 with a more observationally-oriented account. Cosmology in ED is the long-scale evolution of temporal tension across ED gradients:

- **Cosmic expansion** = cumulative temporal tension accumulating across ED gradients (not metric stretching).
- **Redshift** = cumulative participation stretching (gradient-integrated effect, not Doppler/metric).
- **Acceleration** = steepening of ED gradients over time.
- **Structure formation** = amplification of ED variations.
- **Horizons** = global participation limits (not geometric boundaries).
- **Early universe** = high-ED, fully-coupled state (NOT singularity).
- **Inflation-like behavior** = transition from global coherence to event-structure complexity outpacing event-production capacity.

Maps ED gradients onto FRW-like behavior *without* treating the metric as fundamental.

### ED-09 + ED-09.5 вҖ” Quantum behavior and the quantum-classical boundary (Feb 2026)

**ED-09** is the foundational quantum-emergence paper. Quantum behavior arises in low-ED regimes where systems lack the becoming needed to individuate. The vocabulary the ED-I-13 Quantum Information paper uses for specific algorithms originates here:

| Quantum concept | ED mechanism |
|---|---|
| Superposition | Coexisting participation channels |
| Interference | Relational timing between channels |
| Entanglement | Shared participation bandwidth |
| Decoherence | Participation thinning |
| Measurement | Structural commitment to a single stable channel |
| Wavefunction | Coarse-grained summary of participation structure (not a physical object) |

**ED-09.5 is the more interesting paper** because it makes a potentially testable novel prediction. ED posits **two independent phenomena** at the quantum-classical boundary:

1. **Environmental decoherence** вҖ” the standard smooth erosion of coherence by coupling to an environment. ED accepts this.
2. **The ED transition** вҖ” a *sharp structural boundary* determined by internal event density. When a system's internal complexity outpaces its event-production capacity, participation channels collapse to a single stable configuration. **This is not dynamical collapse, not branching, not environmental.** It is a structural limit of becoming.

Standard quantum mechanics predicts only (1) and describes the quantum-classical transition as smooth. ED-09.5 predicts an additional **sharp** transition at a system-dependent internal-complexity threshold.

> **This is a candidate falsifiable prediction that the repo does not currently mention.** If experimentally confirmed, it would be evidence for ED-specific structure beyond standard QM. If the quantum-classical transition is verified to be smooth under all preparations where (1) is controlled for, ED-09.5 is falsified. Worth flagging to the user next time quantum-foundations or macroscopic quantum behavior comes up.

### ED-13 вҖ” Event Density as a Physical Ontology (March 2026) вҖ” the master synthesis

The most integrated empirical statement in the PhilArchive set, and the one most directly usable as a reference for the physics program.

**Architectural claim:** From four primitives and seven axioms, the framework yields a unique scalar dynamical equation whose three channels correspond exactly to familiar physical laws:

- Nonlinear diffusion (mobility channel / porous-medium equation)
- Exponential relaxation (penalty channel / Debye-like)
- Telegraph-type oscillation (participation channel / RLC-like)

**Empirical results reported:**

- **Condensed matter:** Diffusivity decline near saturation fits three chemically distinct systems with a common exponent near 2. Porous-medium front-propagation law confirmed in simulation. (Anchors the UDM result.)
- **Galactic:** ED equation coupled to Poisson gravity produces naturally cored halo profiles matching observed dwarf-galaxy cores. Flat weak-lensing velocities to 1 Mpc via the participation mode interpretation. BTFR reproduced with the observed `1/4` exponent.

**Two sharp discriminating predictions that distinguish ED from CDM and MOND:**

1. **Activity-dependent weak-lensing velocities** вҖ” galaxies with more collective activity should show higher `V_вҲһ` at fixed baryonic mass. (This is the galaxy-level version of the prediction ED-XX later reframes as environment-level.)
2. **Diffusive lensing lag in merging clusters** вҖ” the ED analogue of the merger-lag wake signature. (This is the prediction Cluster Merger-Lag operationalized as `в„“ = D_T / v_current`.)

ED-13 is in a sense the PhilArchive counterpart to the repo's Cluster Merger-Lag + UDM + Dimensional Atlas trio вҖ” it covers the same empirical ground in condensed single-paper form. When a future session needs a one-reference citation for the empirical physics program, ED-13 is the paper.

### ED-03 вҖ” Extensions of Event Density: Structural Consequences Across Physics (Feb 2026)

The cross-domain overview that preceded the deeper treatments in ED-10 (spacetime), ED-09 (quantum), ED-06 (horizons), ED-08 (cosmology). Four domains treated:

1. **Gravitation** вҖ” curvature = macroscopic geometry of ED flow.
2. **Quantum mechanics** вҖ” quantum behavior in low-ED regimes.
3. **Information / entropy** вҖ” complementary ED expressions; holography from ED gradient concentration at boundaries.
4. **Cosmology** вҖ” long-scale ED evolution.

Qualitative, less developed than the domain-specific papers that followed. Useful as the introductory overview; skipable if ED-10 + ED-09 + ED-06 + ED-08 are already in hand.

### 5.6 ED-Math-01 вҖ” Uniqueness theorem and the nine architectural laws L1вҖ“L9

**Source:** `Desktop/ED Important Papers/ED-Math-01_Uniqueness_Well-Posedness_and_Architectural_Laws.md`. Read 2026-04-21. This is the **formal mathematical layer** of ED вҖ” the document that turns the PDE canon into a theorem.

**Theorem 2.1 (Uniqueness).** The canonical ED PDE is the unique second-order scalar PDE satisfying the seven *derivation* axioms (В§3.1). Proof by constructive elimination: P1+P2 reduce the operator to functions of `(ПҒ, |вҲҮПҒ|ВІ, вҲҮВІПҒ)`; P3 determines the principal part; P4 constrains the reaction term; P5 excludes non-scalar fields; P6 determines the coupling form; P7 ensures dimension-independence. Combined with ED-05's pre-PDE axioms and the Canon's structural principles, this provides a closed derivation of the ED PDE from first principles вҖ” **no tuning, no fit, no free choice of form**.

**Well-posedness results** (proved per-channel in ED-Math-01):

| Channel | Well-posedness theorem | Condition |
|:---|:---|:---|
| Mobility (PME reduction) | Existence and uniqueness of weak solutions | Follows from VГЎzquez (2007) once the `M(ПҒ) вҶ’ 0` degeneracy is confined to the capacity bound |
| Penalty (RC reduction) | Global-in-time regularity | `P'(ПҒ*) > 0` (monotone attractor) |
| Participation (coupled ODE-PDE) | Existence via linear superposition onto the mobility+penalty solution | Requires finite `П„`, `О¶ > 0` |

**The nine architectural laws L1вҖ“L9** (ED-Math-01, also summarized in the Desktop `ED Laws All so far.PNG`). These are *consequences* of the Canon вҖ” things every architecturally-ED PDE must exhibit:

| # | Law | Statement |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **L1** | Unique attractor | The penalty channel defines a unique, globally attracting equilibrium `ПҒ*` |
| **L2** | Energy monotonicity | Multiple simultaneous Lyapunov functionals decay monotonically (gradient, entropy, energy, penalty, participation) |
| **L3** | Spectral concentration | Solutions concentrate onto a low-dimensional invariant spectrum (3-stage convergence theorem) |
| **L4** | Factorial complexity dilution | Mode coupling dilutes as `1/k!`, so high-k structure damps rapidly |
| **L5** | GradientвҖ“dissipation dominance | At late times, dissipation rate tracks `вҖ–вҲҮПҒвҖ–ВІ` вҖ” the gradient is the ledger |
| **L6** | Topological conservation | Horizon topology is preserved under smooth ED evolution (no spontaneous horizon birth in the parabolic regime) |
| **L7** | Horizon formation | For `ПҒ > ПҒ_crit`, mobility degenerates and a free boundary (transient horizon) forms |
| **L8** | Morphological hierarchy | Hessian eigenvalue morphology follows blobs вҶ’ filaments вҶ’ sheets вҶ’ uniform (confirmed in 2D/3D by ED-SIM-3D В§6.7) |
| **L9** | SheetвҖ“filament oscillation | In the oscillatory regime (D < 0.1), sheet and filament morphologies interconvert via telegraph oscillations |

These hold across dimensions d = 1вҖ“4 (L7вҖ“L9 are partially dimension-dependent per ED-SIM-3D). **Relationship to the Canon:** the L-laws are *theorems* about systems that satisfy the Canon's P-principles, not additional axioms. L1 вҶ” P3; L7 вҶ” P4; L9 вҶ” P5+P6; etc. When a session needs a single reference for the formal mathematical status of the ED PDE, ED-Math-01 is it.

### 5.7 The six structural analogues (Foundational Paper v2)

**Source:** `Desktop/ED Important Papers/ED_Foundational_Paper_v2.md`. Read 2026-04-21. This is the **empirical-structural layer** of the Foundational Paper вҖ” six minimal experiments that isolate or combine the three ED channels and check whether the resulting dynamics match a known physical law. This is what makes ED *falsifiable* at the structural level.

| # | Channels exercised | Physical law | Key result |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **1** | Penalty only | RC / Debye exponential decay | `О» = DPвӮҖ` matched to **0.00%** (machine precision) including RLC frequencies `Пү` at H = 0.3, 1.0, 5.0 |
| **2** | Mobility only | Barenblatt PME `вҲӮ_t Оҙ = D_pme вҲҮВІ(Оҙ^m)` with `m = ОІ+1` | `Оұ_R = 1/(d(m-1)+2)` matched to **1.1%** at ОІ=1; pre-asymptotic at ОІ=2, 3; compact support confirmed |
| **3** | Mobility + Penalty | Stefan free-boundary / transient horizons | Sharp amplitude threshold `A_c = 0.400` predicted, measured `0.410` (**2.5%**); horizon lifetime monotonic in A |
| **4** | All three | Oscillatory horizon modulation | **Scientifically informative negative result.** Horizons are too short-lived (`П„_H ~ 0.3вҖ“1.5`) relative to the telegraph period (`T_osc ~ 2вҖ“6`) for boundary oscillation. Structural consequence of L1 (unique attractor) вҖ” not a numerical artifact |
| **5** | Mobility + Participation | Telegraph-modulated PME | `Пү вҲқ H^{0.52}` (predicted `H^{0.50}`, within 4%); vвҖ“Оҙ frequency match to **0.03%** at H = 50. Also surfaced the structural identity `bar{F} = 0` when `PвӮҖ = 0` under Neumann BC вҖ” participation needs penalty to activate |
| **6** | All three (two-peak) | Emergent pair interaction | **Discovered** nonlinear-mobility repulsion (not anticipated analytically): tail overlap вҶ’ lower local mobility вҶ’ outer-edge-faster spreading вҶ’ centres drift apart. Telegraph coupling at H > 0 modulates this between attraction and repulsion (correlation ~ +0.5 with v(t)) |

**What the six analogues establish:** Each channel corresponds *exactly* (not approximately) to a known physical law at the level of governing equations. The penalty *is* RC discharge; the mobility *is* porous-medium diffusion; the participation *is* a telegraph oscillator. Channel combinations produce higher-level structure (horizons, modulated spreading, effective pair interactions) that is richer than the sum of the individual channels. The one negative result (Analogue 4) is a structural consequence of L1 and is informative, not a failure.

**3D validation (Appendix_G_3D_Analogues.md, read 2026-04-21).** Three of the six analogues (Barenblatt, Horizon, Temporal Tension) were re-run in 3D. All three structural patterns extend to 3D without modification; only numerical parameters shift per the `d`-dependent Laplacian:
- Barenblatt: `Оұ_R = 1/(d(m-1)+2)` predicts `Оұ_R = 0.2` for d=3, ОІ=1; measured `0.1665` (16.7% pre-asymptotic error, same pattern as 2D at ОІ=2). Compact support confirmed.
- Horizon threshold: `A_c` shifts from `0.41` (2D) to `0.45` (3D), consistent with Laplacian-at-peak scaling `вҲ’dA/ПғВІ` вҖ” 3D dissipates the peak 50% faster.
- Temporal tension: baseline nonlinear-mobility repulsion present in all runs; telegraph-modulated reversal at H = 2 preserved; v-correlation exceeds 0.67 at H = 5. Drift rates slightly lower in 3D than 2D, consistent with solid-angle distribution of tail overlap.

**Axiom P7 (dimensional consistency) is thus empirically validated** вҖ” the same constitutive channels produce the same structural analogues in any dimension, with numerical parameters shifting only through the geometry of the Laplacian.

### 5.8 ED-Dimensional-01 Quantum Regime вҖ” the first anchored cross-scale mapping

**Source:** `Desktop/ED Important Papers/ED-Dimensional-01_Quantum_Regime.md`. Read 2026-04-21. This is the **first** of the five regime mappings (the others are Planck, condensed matter, galactic, cosmological). The quantum regime is chosen first because it has the strongest anchoring: `D_phys = в„Ҹ/(2m)` is determined by a **mathematical theorem** (the Madelung transformation of the SchrГ¶dinger equation), not by physical analogy or experimental fit. Every other regime requires at least one parameter to be set by convention or measurement.

**Three characteristic scales (anchoring):**

| Scale | Formula | Origin |
|:---|:---|:---|
| `L_0` | `в„Ҹ/(mc)` (reduced Compton wavelength) | Smallest length where single-particle probability density is meaningful |
| `D_phys` | `в„Ҹ/(2m)` | **Madelung theorem** вҖ” the free-particle SchrГ¶dinger equation rewritten as a continuity equation for `|ПҲ|ВІ` has this exact coefficient. Not an analogy |
| `T_0` | `LвӮҖВІВ·D_nd / D_phys = 2В·D_ndВ·в„Ҹ/(mcВІ) = 0.6В·в„Ҹ/(mcВІ)` for `D_nd = 0.3` | Derived; вүҲ 0.6Г— Compton time |

**Superluminal `V_0 = c/(2В·D_nd) = 1.667c`.** This is **not a physical velocity.** It is a scale conversion factor, a mathematical consequence of the parabolic nature of the PDE. The ED equation and the SchrГ¶dinger equation share this property: both are parabolic with infinite propagation speed; neither respects a causal light cone. A relativistic hyperbolic extension would be required for causal propagation. Treat `V_0` as a regime-boundary marker, never as a signal speed.

**The ED-to-quantum dictionary** (full table in the source document; key rows):

| ED parameter | Physical quantity | Status |
|:---|:---|:---|
| `ПҒ` | `|ПҲ|ВІ` probability density | Anchored (via `R_0 = LвӮҖ^{-d}` so that `вҲ«ПҒ` over `LвӮҖ^d` = 1) |
| `D` = 0.3 | Quantum diffusivity `в„Ҹ/(2m)` | **Exact** (Madelung theorem) |
| `M(ПҒ) = MвӮҖ(1-ПҒМӮ)^ОІ` | Density-dependent probability-diffusion slowing | **ED-specific prediction** вҖ” distinguishes ED from standard QM |
| `P(ПҒ)` | Restoring force (confining-potential analogue) | Anchored |
| `v(t)` | Mean-field / decoherence mode amplitude | Candidate |
| `П„` | Decoherence timescale | Candidate |
| `H` | Environmental / measurement coupling | Candidate |
| `ОІ = 2` | Mobility exponent (PME index `m = ОІ + 1 = 3`) | Structural constitutive choice |

**Numerical values for the electron (d = 2):** `LвӮҖ = 3.862Г—10вҒ»В№Ві m`, `TвӮҖ = 7.729Г—10вҒ»ВІВІ s`, `D_phys = 5.788Г—10вҒ»вҒө mВІ/s`. Planck-mass row recovers the Planck scales вҖ” the quantum and Planck regimes are connected by a single parameter (the particle mass).

**ED's strongest prediction / weakest link in the quantum regime** is the density-dependent mobility `M(ПҒ) = MвӮҖ(1 - ПҒМӮ)^ОІ`. Standard QM has constant diffusion. ED predicts probability-density transport **slows as `ПҒ вҶ’ ПҒ_max`** (analogous to Pauli blocking / nonlinear SchrГ¶dinger dynamics). If observed, this distinguishes ED from standard QM. If no density-dependent slowing is ever observed in quantum systems, `ОІ > 0` is falsified in this regime. No experimental evidence currently supports or refutes this prediction; it is the most testable distinguishing feature.

**Cross-regime validation** (ED-Dimensional-Master, read 2026-04-21): the universal nondimensional invariant `D_phys В· TвӮҖ / LвӮҖВІ = 0.3` holds to machine precision across all five regimes вҖ” Quantum (`LвӮҖ = в„Ҹ/mc`, `D = в„Ҹ/2m`), Planck (`LвӮҖ = в„“_Pl`, `D = вҲҡ(в„ҸG/c)`), Condensed matter (user-fit, ~Ојm and thermal diffusivity), Galactic (1 kpc, `D_T = 2.1Г—10ВІвҒ· mВІ/s`), Cosmological (`c/HвӮҖ` and `ПҒ_crit`). This is 61 orders of magnitude in length scale and the same invariant holds throughout. The structure-growth problem at cosmological scale (the monostable penalty cannot generate cosmic structure growth on its own) is flagged as the most fundamental open question of the ED program.

### 5.9 ED-Phys вҖ” The Architecture of Physical Law: Symmetry, Constraint, and Emergent Regularity

**Source:** PhilArchive, title *Event Density and the Architecture of Physical Law: Symmetry, Constraint, and Emergent Regularity*. Discovered in the 2026-04-21 PhilArchive survey; not on Desktop under this name. This paper is **philosophically central** to the ED program and had not been captured in prior orientation drafts.

**Central claim.** Physics typically treats its laws, symmetries, and conserved quantities as **fundamental features of the universe** вҖ” they are what *must* be true, and everything else is what *happens* to be true. The ED framework inverts this: laws, symmetries, and conservation quantities are **emergent architectural consequences** of ED structure (gradients, participation relations, compositional rule, decoupling surfaces), **not fundamental postulates**. Physics's laws are *what must emerge when the architecture is what it is*, not what must be stipulated.

**What the paper re-derives as emergent (rather than fundamental):**

| Standard framing | ED framing |
|:---|:---|
| Noether's theorem: symmetry вҶ’ conservation law | Conservation emerges from invariance of ED gradients under participation-preserving transformations. Symmetries are architectural, not postulated. |
| Gauge invariance as fundamental | Gauge structure emerges from the redundancy of participation rules in ED-channel geometry (ED-I-14 / ED-I-13 interpretation). Not postulated; arises from the fact that identity alignment is a structural rather than substantive commitment. |
| Lorentz symmetry as a fundamental spacetime symmetry | Lorentz symmetry is a structural consequence of participation architecture (ED-07). Not a geometric axiom. |
| Conservation of energy / momentum | Emerges from the irreversibility of commitment (ED-10 В§6) combined with the architectural constraint that committed micro-events cannot be unmade. |
| Time-translation invariance | Equivalent to the architectural claim that the compositional rule is stationary вҖ” which is itself a consequence of the pre-PDE axioms' subadditivity (ED-05 В§4). |
| Second law of thermodynamics | Follows structurally from the monotone descent of the ED Lyapunov functionals (Law L2 of В§5.6) and the irreversibility of commitment (ED-10 В§6). |
| Constants of nature (c, в„Ҹ, G, Оұ...) | Not arbitrary fine-tunings. The dimensional atlas (В§5.8) anchors each constant to a regime-specific structural quantity (`D_phys В· TвӮҖ / LвӮҖВІ = 0.3` across 61 orders of magnitude). |

**Why this paper matters for orientation.** It is the **meta-claim that unifies the three ED tracks** documented at the top of this doc:

- **Empirical track** (UDM, Cluster Merger-Lag, BTFR, dwarf D_outer): tests *specific* emergent regularities.
- **Interpretive track** (ED-I-12/13/14/27): reinterprets *specific* phenomena (photonics, quantum info, topology, weak lensing) as ED-channel manipulations.
- **Scale-correspondence track** (ED-SC): identifies *architectural invariants* that recur across scales.

The Architecture-of-Physical-Law paper is **the philosophical claim behind all three tracks**: the reason any of these work is that physical "law" is itself emergent from architecture. When a session encounters a question like "why is physics governed by these specific laws?" or "why should ED be a candidate theory of *everything*, not just a theory of *dark matter*?" вҖ” this paper is the reference. The empirical, interpretive, and scale-correspondence tracks all presuppose its central claim.

**How this connects to the Emergence-Universe sandbox (В§11).** The ED-SIM sandbox is the **empirical demonstration** of this paper's philosophical claim: in a deterministic minimal universe where the architecture is known and explicit, the 14 laws IвҖ“XIV emerge inevitably. No randomness, no external forcing, no imposed symmetries вҖ” the laws are "the walls, and the physical laws we observe are just the shape of the space trapped inside them" (README verbatim). The Generative Closure theorem (Law XIII: exactly 10 sub-mechanism types, no 11th possible) is the sandbox-level proof that the architecture *forbids alternatives* вҖ” which is the same claim the Architecture-of-Physical-Law paper makes for our universe.

**Reading-order placement.** For a new session, this paper sits between ED-10 (emergence map) and ED-13 (master empirical synthesis). It is the *why* behind ED-10's coarse-graining dictionary: why space, time, curvature, and horizons are architectural outputs, not metaphysical inputs.

## 6. The environment-sourcing revision (ED-XX April 2026) вҖ” MOST IMPORTANT UPDATE

### What the ED-XX 3D argument showed

> **Attribution note.** Earlier drafts of this orientation called this "what ED-Sim-01 showed." That attribution is wrong вҖ” the actual ED-Sim-01 paper is the Scenario-D architectural-invariants experiment (В§6.8), which contains no Green's-function derivation. The 1/r dilution argument's source document is still unlocated; the summary below is reconstructed from ED-XX's own Table (see В§6, "Numerical scan") and is presumed to live inside the ED-XX paper itself.

- The 3D steady-state Green's function of the temporal-tension PDE is `T(r) вҲқ (1/r)В·exp(вҲ’r/в„“_T)`.
- **The `1/r` geometric dilution dominates long before exponential decay kicks in.** This is a geometric fact of 3D, absent in 1D.
- A compact galactic source (5вҖ“20 kpc) cannot produce a flat `T(r)` over the 10вҖ“1000 kpc range required by rotation curves / weak lensing вҖ” regardless of `в„“_T`. The 1D intuition that motivated ED-02 and ED-04 fails in 3D.
- Flatness at 30вҖ“1000 kpc requires source width `Пғ вүҘ 1вҖ“3 Mpc`.

### Numerical scan (from ED-XX Table)

| Source width Пғ | Flatness error over 30вҖ“1000 kpc |
|---:|---:|
| 5 kpc | 258% |
| 50 kpc | 71% |
| 500 kpc | 18% |
| 1000 kpc | 6.8% |
| 2000 kpc | **2.7%** |

### What this changes

- Galaxies (5вҖ“20 kpc): too small to source their own flat temporal-tension halos.
- Galaxy groups (0.5вҖ“2 Mpc), filaments (5вҖ“50 Mpc), local cosmic web: the correct source scale.
- **Role split:** the galaxy sets the *amplitude* (via its baryonic identity and internal event density); the environment sets the *spatial extent* (via megaparsec-scale collective activity).

### New predictions that distinguish ED from both CDM and MOND

1. **Activity-dependent weak-lensing velocities** вҖ” `V_вҲһ вҲқ вҲҡS_env`, not `M_halo^(1/3)` (CDM) and not MOND's `a_0` threshold.
2. **Environmental coherence** вҖ” galaxies in the same group/filament share asymptotic V: `V_вҲһ^(i) вүҲ V_вҲһ^(j)`. Incompatible with CDM (which gives each galaxy its own halo).
3. **No halo edge** вҖ” field is scale-free, no virial truncation.
4. **No MOND transition radius** вҖ” no `a = a_0` crossover.
5. **Merger-lag signatures preserved** вҖ” cluster mergers ARE the environmental source at cluster scale, so Cluster Merger-Lag work is unaffected.

### Implications for repo-level work

- **BTFR-activity test (ED-Data-12..17 + `papers/ED-BTFR-Activity/memo.md`)** вҖ” was testing galaxy-level ПҒ(sSFR, О”_BTFR). Under ED-XX the proper variable is *environmental* activity, not individual-galaxy sSFR. Individual-galaxy sSFR correlates with environmental activity but imperfectly; signal is diluted. BIG-SPARC with group/filament cross-match is the right path.
- **Dwarf D_outer (ED-04.5)** вҖ” still stands. Qualitative "active" morphology correlates with environmental activity, so the 53% separation survives as an environmental proxy.
- **RLC analogue memo** вҖ” unaffected; tests the PDE's uniform-limit coupling structure, not what sources the field.
- **Cluster Merger-Lag** вҖ” unaffected; clusters are environmental sources already.
- **ED-I-27 weak-lensing interpretation** вҖ” written March 2026 under galaxy-sourced framing. Its core claim (weak lensing detects temporal-tension field, not mass) survives; what changes is the source identification.
